॥1॥ atha niyukti-pīṭhikā ॥
॥ atha sāmāyikākhyaṁ prathamamadhyayanam ॥
ābhiṇibōhiyanāṇaṁ, suyanāṇaṁ cēva ōhināṇaṁ ca ।
taha maraṇapajjava (ya)nāṇaṁ, kēvala nāṇaṁ ca paṁcamayaṁ ॥ 1।।
10 ugahō īhā'vāō ya dhāraṇā ēva hum̐ti cattāri ।
ābhiṇibōhiyanāṇassa bhēyavatthū samāsēṇaṁ ।। 2 ।।
atthāṇaṁ uggahaṇaṁ avaggahaṁ taha viprālaṇaṁ ihaṁ ।
vavasāyaṁ ca avāyaṁ dharaṇaṁ puṇa dhāraṇaṁ bēti ।। 3 ।।
(asthāṇaṁ prōgahaṇāmmi uggahō taha viyāra (la)ṇē īhā ।
15 vavasāyammi pravāō dharaṇaṁ puṇa dhāraṇaṁ bēṁti 3 )
uggaha ikkaṁ samayaṁ īhā'vāyā muttamaddhaṁ (maṁta) tu ।

kattō mē vaṇṇē, sattī prōhissa savvapayaḍīmō ?
caudasavihanikkhēvaṁ, iḍḍīpattē ya vōcchāmi ।। 26 ।।
ōhi khittaparimāṇē, saṁṭhāṇē prāṇugāmiē ।
avaṭṭhiē calē tibvamaṁdapaḍivāuppayā ia ।। 27 ।।
5 nāṇadaṁsaṇavibhaṁgē, dēsē khittē gaī ina ।
iḍḍhīpattāṇuprōgē ya, ēmēā paḍivattīprō ।। 28 ।।
nāma ṭhavaṇādaviē, khittē kālē bhavē ya bhāvē ya ।
ēsō khalu nikkhēvō, ōhissā hōi sattavihō ।। 29 ।।
jāvaiyā tisamayāhāragassa suhumassa paṇagajīvassa ।
10 ōgāhaṇā jahaṇṇā, ōhōkhittaṁ jahaṇṇaṁ tu ॥ 30 ।।
savvabahuagaṇijīvā, niraṁtaraṁ jattiyaṁ bharijjaṁsu ।
khittaṁ savadisāgaṁ, paramōhī khitta niddiṭṭō ।। 31 ।।
aṁgulamāvaliyāṇaṁ, bhāgamasaṁkhijja dōsu saṁkhijjā।
aṁgulamāvalitō, prāvalimā aṁgulapuhuttaṁ ।। 32 ।।
15 hatthaṁmi muhuttaṁtō, divasaṁtō gāuaṁmi bōddhavyō ।
jōyaṇa divasaputrā, pakkhaṁtō pagṇavīsānō ॥ 33 ॥
bharahami addhamāsō, jaṁbūdīvaṁmi sāhiyō māsō ।
vāsaṁ ca maṇupralōē, vāsapuhuttaṁ ca ruyagaṁmi ॥ 34 ॥
saṁkhijjami u kālē, dōvasamuddā ya hum̐ti saṁkhijjā ।
20 kālaṁmi prasaṁkhijjē, dōvasamuddā u bhaiyavvā ॥ 35 ।।
kālē cauṇha vuḍḍī, kālō bhaiyavvu khittavr̥ḍḍīē ।
vuḍḍōī davapajjava, bhaiyatvā khittakālā u ।। 36 ।।

1 sāmāyikādhyayanam :: 2-upōdghātaniyuktiḥ ] [ 9
॥ 2॥ athōpōdghātaniyuktiḥ ।।
titthayarē bhagavaṁtē, aṇuttaraparakkamē amiyanāṇī ।
tiṇṇē sugaigaiē, siddhipahapadēsagaē vaṁdē ।। 80 ।।
vaṁdāmi mahābhāga, mahāmuṇi mahāyasaṁ mahāvīraṁ ।
amaranararāyamāhiyaṁ, titthayaramimassa titthassa ।। 81 ।।
ikkārasavi gaṇaharē, pavāyaē pavayaṇassa dāmi ।
savvaṁ gaṇaharavaṁsaṁ vāyagavaṁsaṁ pavayaraṇaṁ ca ।। 82 ॥
tē vaṁdiūṇa sirasā prasthapuhuttassa tēhi kahiyassa ।
suyanāṇassa bhagavaō, 'nijjutti kittaissāmi ॥23॥
10 āvassagassa dasakāliassa taha uttarajjhamāyārē ।
sūyagaḍē nijjutti vucchāmi tahā dasāṇaṁ ca ।। 84 ॥
kappassa ya nijjutti, vavahārassēva paramaṇi ṇassa ।
sūriapaṇṇattīē, vucchaṁ isibhāsiyāṇaṁ ca
ētēsi nijjutti, vucchāmi ahaṁ jiṇōvaēsēṇaṁ ।
15 prāharaṇahēukāraṇa-payanivahamiṇaṁ samāsēṇaṁ ॥86 ।।
sāmāiyanijjutti, vucchaṁ uvaēsiyaṁ gurujaṇēṇaṁ ।
āyariyaparaṁparaēṇa, āgayaṁ āṇupuvīē
nijjuttā tē pratthā, jaṁ baddhā tēṇa hōi ṇijjuttī,
(ahavā suyaparivāḍī suōvayēsō'yaṁ viśēṣā)।
20 tahavi ya icchāvēi, vibhāsiuṁ suttaparivāḍī ।। 88 ।।
tavaniyamanāṇarukkhaṁ, ārūḍhō kēvalī amiyanāṇī ।
।। 85 ।।

[ niyuktisaṁgraha :: 1 āvaśyakaniyuktiḥ
10
tō muyai nāṇavuṣṭhiṁ, bhaviyajaṇavibōhaṇaṭṭhāē ॥ 86 ॥
taṁ buddhimaēṇa paḍēṇa, gaṇaharā gihi niravasēsaṁ ।
titthayarabhāsiyāī, gaṁthaṁti taō pavayaṇaṭṭhā ।। 60 ।।
ghittuca suhaṁ suhaguṇa (gaha) ṇadhāraṇā dāuṁ pucchiuṁ cēva ।
5 ēēhi kāraṇēhiṁ, jīyaṁti kayaṁ gaṇaharēhiṁ ।। 91 ।।
pratthaṁ bhāsai arahā, suttaṁ gaṁthaṁti gaṇaharā niurṇa ।
( gaṇadharā nipuṇā, niguṇā )
sāsaṇassa hiyaṭṭāē, tō suttaṁ titthaṁ pavattai ।। 92 ॥
sāmāiyamāīyaṁ suyanāṇaṁ jāva biṁdusārāō ।
tassavi sārō caraṇaṁ, sārō caraṇassa nivvāṇaṁ ।। 93 ।।
suyanāṇaṁmi vi jīvō, baṭṭatō sō na pāuṇai mōkkhaṁ ।
jō tavasaṁjamamaiē jōē na caēi vōḍhuṁ jē ॥64 ।।
jaha chēyaladdhanijjāmō'vi, vāṇiyagaicchiyaṁ bhūmi ।
vāēga viṇā pōō, na caēi mahaṇṇavaṁ tariuṁ ।। 65 ।।
15 taha nāṇaladdhanijjāmanō'vi, siddhivasahi na pāuṇai ।
niuṇō'vi jīvapōō, tavasaṁjamamārupravihūṇō ॥66 ।।
saṁsārasāgarāpō, ubbuḍḍō mā puṇō nibuḍḍijjā ।
caraṇaguṇavippahīṇō, buḍḍai subahuṁpi jāṇatō ।। 67 ।।
subahum̐pi suyamahīyaṁ, ki kāhī? caraṇavippahīṇa (mukka)ssa ।
20 aṁdhassa jaha palittā, dīvasayasahassakōḍīvi ।। 8 ।।
appaṁpi suyamahīyaṁ, payāsayaṁ hōi caraṇajuttassa ।
ikkō'vi jaha paīvō, sacakkhuassā payāsēi ।। 66 ।।

praddhaṭṭhamā sahassā aḍḍāijjā ya satta ya sayāī ।

aha taṁ pāgaḍarūvaṁ vaṭhṭhapucchēi (pucchisu) bahujaṇō dhamma ।

[ niyuktisaṁgrahaḥ :: (1) āvaśyaka niyuktiḥ
bārasa
chammāṇi gōva kaḍasala pavēsaṇaṁ majjhimāē pāvāē ।
kharaō vijja siddhastha vāṇiyānō nōharāvēi ।। 25 ।।

5 jō ya tavō aṇuciṣṇō vīravarēṇaṁ mahāṇubhāvēṇaṁ ।
chaumatthakāliyāē ahakkama kittaissāmi ॥ 27 ।।
nava kira cāummāsē chakkīra dōmāsiē uvāsīya ।
ya māsiyāī bāvattari addhamāsāiṁ ॥ 28 ॥
ēga kira chammāsaṁ dō kira tēmāsiē uvāsīya ।
10 aḍḍāijjā ya duvē dō cēva divaḍḍamāsāī ।। 29 ।।

dō cattāri dasēva ya divasē ṭhāsīya aṇubaddhaṁ ।। 530 ॥
gōyaramabhiggahajuyaṁ khamaṇaṁ chammāsiyaṁ ca kāsī ya ।
paṁcadivasēhi ūṇaṁ avvāhiō vacchana yarīē ।। 31 ॥
dasa dō ya kira mahappā ṭhāi muṇī ēgarāiyaṁ paḍimaṁ ।
aṭṭhamabhattēṇa jaī ēkkēkkaṁ caramarāīyaṁ ॥ 32 ॥

5 tē pavvaiē sōuṁ akaṁpinō āgacchaī jiṇasagāsaṁ ।
baccāmi vaṁdāmī vaṁdittā pajjuvāsāmi ॥ 26 ।।
āmaṭṭō ya jiṇēṇaṁ jāijarāmaraṇavippamukkēṇaṁ ।
nāmēṇa ya gōttēṇa ya samvaṣṇū savvadarisīṇaṁ ।। 27 ।।
ki mannē nēraiyā asthi na asthitti saṁsaō tujjhaṁ ।
10 vēyapayāṇa ya atthaṁ ṇa yāṇasī tēsimō pratthō ।। 28 ॥
chinnaṁmi saṁsayaṁmī jiṇēṇa jaramaraṇavippamukkēṇaṁ ।
sō samaṇō pavaiō tihi u saha khaṁḍiyasaēhiṁ ।। 29 ।।
tē pavvaiē sōuṁ ayalabhāyā āgacchaha jigasagāsaṁ ।
vaccāmi ṇa vaṁdāmī vaṁdittā pajjuvāsāmi ।। 630 ।।
15 ābhaṭṭhō ya jiṇēṇaṁ jāijarāmaraṇaviṣpamukkēṇaṁ ।
nāmēṇa ya gōttēṇa ya savvaṇṇū savvadarisōṇaṁ ।। 31 ।।
ki manni pugṇapāvaṁ asthi na asthitti saṁsaō tujhaṁ ।
vēyapayāṇa ya pratthaṁ raṇa yāṇasī tēsimō atthō ।। 32 ।।
chiṇṇami saṁsayaṁmī jiṇēṇa jaramaraṇavippamukkēṇaṁ ।
20 sō samaṇō pavvaiyō tihi u saha khaṁḍiyasaēhiṁ ।। 33 ।।
tē padhvaiē sōuṁ mēyajjō āgacchai jiṇasagāsaṁ ।
vaccāmi ṇa vaṁdāmī vaṁdittā pajjuvāsāmi ॥ 34 ।।

caurō'vi tivihavēdē ca usuvi saṇṇāsu hōi paḍivattī ।

caurō'vi tivihajōgē uvaōgadugaṁmi caura paḍivajjē ।
pōrāliē caukkaṁ sammasuya viuviē bhayaṇā ।। 820 ।।

gabbhagaē jaṁ jaṇaṇō jāya supāsā tō supāsajiṇō।

samvavihīsu pra kusalā gabhagaē tēṇa hōi suvihijiṇō।
piuṇō dāhōvasamō gabbhagaē sīyalō tēṇaṁ ॥97 ॥
maharihasijjārahaṇaṁmi dōhalō tēṇa hōha sijjaṁsō ।
20 pūēi vāsavō jaṁ abhikkhaṇaṁ tēṇa vasupujjō ॥98॥
vimalataṇubuddhi jaṇaṇī gabhagaē tēṇa hōi vimalajiṇō।

assiṇi kattiya miyasira pussō maha pharaguhattha citā ya ।

taha rēvaitti ēē pannarasa havaṁti tīsa imuhuttā ।
nāyavvā pariḍhavaṇavihīya kusalēṇaṁ ॥ 44 ।।
sabhisayā bharaṇīō addā assēsa sāi jēṭṭhā ya ।

aṇarāyaē ya sabhaē jaccira niddōcca'hōrattaṁ ।। 58 ।।
sēṇāhivaī bhōiya mayaharasithimallajuddha ya ।
lōṭṭāibhaṁḍaṇē vā gujjhaga uḍḍāhamaciyat ।। 56 ।।
taddivasabhōiāī aṁtō sattaṇha jāva sajjhāō।
10 aṇahassa ya hatthasayaṁ diṭṭhi vivittami suddhaṁ tu ।। 1360 ॥
mayaharapagaē bahupakkhiē ya sattaghara aṁtaramaē vā ।
nidda khatti ya garihā na paḍhaṁti saṇīyagaṁ vāvi ।। 61 ।।
sāgāriyāi kahaṇaṁ aṇiccha ratti vasahā vigi caṁti ।
vikkinnē va samatā jaṁ diṭṭha saḍhēyarē suddhā ।। 62 ।।
15 sārīrapi ya duvihaṁ māṇusa tēricchiyaṁ samāsēṇaṁ ।
tēricchaṁ tattha tihā jalathalakhahajaṁ ca uddhā u
paṁcidiyāṇa davē khēttē saṭṭhihattha puggalāinna ।
tikurattha mahaṁtēgā nagarē bāhiṁ tu gāmassa
kālē tipōrasi'ḍha va bhāvē sutaṁ tu naṁdimāīyaṁ ।
sōṇiya maṁsaṁ cammaṁ aṭṭhī viya hum̐ti cattāri ।। 65 ।।
aṁtō bahiṁ ca dhōaṁ saṭṭhīhatthāu pōrisī tinni ।
mahakāē ahōrattaṁ raddha vuḍḍē ya suddhaṁ tu ।। 66 ।।

asthittibahupaēsā tēṇaṁ paṁcasthikāyā ।। 1450 ।।
tīyamaṇāgayabhāvaṁ jamathikāyāṇa natthi atthit ।
10 tēna ra kēvalaēK natthī davasthikāyataṁ ॥ 51 ।।
kāmaṁ bhaviyasurāisa bhāvō sō cēva jattha vaṭṭati ।
ēssō na tāva jāyai tēna ra tē davvadēvutti ।। 52 ।।
duhaō'ṇaṁtararahiyā jai ēvaṁ tō bhavā aṇaṁtaguṇā ।
ēgassa ēgakālē bhavā na jujjati u aṇēgā ।। 53 ।।
15 duhaprō'ṇaṁtarabhaviyaṁ jaha ciṭṭhai pāugraṁ tu jaṁ baddhaṁ ।
hujjiyarēsuvi jai taṁ davabhavā hujja tō tē'vi ॥ 54 ।।

khīrāigahaṇa dōhum̐ bahuṁ ca uvamā ayakaḍillē ।। 62 ।।
jē cēva paḍicchaṇadīha-khaddhasuvaṇēsu vaṇimā dōsā ।
tē cēva sapaḍivakkhā hōṁti ihaṁ kāraṇajjāē ।। 93 ।।
5 uggamadōsāīṇaṁ kahaṇā uppāyaṇēsaṇāṇaṁ ca
tattha u natthī sunnē bāhiṁ sāgāra kāladuvē ।। 64 ।।
diṭṭhamadiṭṭhā duvihā nāyaguṇā cēva hum̐ti annāyā ।
addiṭṭhāvi duvihā supramasuna pasatthamapasatthā
diṭṭhā va samōsaraṇō na ya nāyaguṇā havējja tē samaṇā ।
10 supraguṇa pasattha iyarē samaṇuniarē ya savvēvi ।। 96 ।।
jai suddhā saṁvāsō hōī asuddhāṇa duviha paḍilēhā ।
abhitarabāhirimā duvihā davē a bhāvē pra ॥ 97 ।।
ghaṭṭhāitaliadaṁḍaga pāuya saṁlaggirī aṇuvaōgō।
disi pavaṇagāmasūria vitahaṁ ucchōlaṇā davē ॥98 ।।
15 vikahā hasiumgāiya bhinnakahācakkavālachaliakahā ।
māṇusa tiriyāvāē dāyaṇaprāyararagayā bhāvē ।। 66 ।।
bāhiṁ jaivi asuddhā tahāvi gaṁtūṇa guruparikkhā u ।
ahava visuddhā tahavi u aṁtō duvihā u paḍilēhā ।।10।।
pavisaṁtani mattaṇēsaṇaṁ va sāhaina ērisā samaṇā ।
20 amhaṁpi tē kahatī kukkuḍakhariyāiṭhāṇaṁ ca ।। 101 ॥
davvaṁmi ṭhāṇaphalaē sējjāsaṁthārakāyauccārē ।
kaṁdappagīyavikahā vuggahakiḍḍā ya
bhāvaṁmi ।। 102 ।।

aibhārēṇa u irigraṁ na sōhaē kaṁṭagāi prāyāē।
20 bhattadvia vōsiriā aiṁtu ēvaṁ jaḍhā dōsā ।। 87 ।।
prāyariavayaṇa dōsā duvihā niyamā u saṁjamāyāē ।
vaccaha na tujjha sāmī asaṁkhaḍaṁ maṁḍalīē vā ॥ 88 ।।

[ niyuktisaṁgrahaḥ :: (2) śrīmatī ōdhaniyuktiḥ
paṁḍaga appaḍisēvī mattō saḍḍhō va appasāgariē ।
khēttāi bha gāṇaṁ karacaraṇa bippasāgariē । 71 ।।
saḍḍhō va annabhaṇa aṁdhē saviyāraṇā ya balumi ।
taddōsiē abhinnē vēlā thaṇajīviyaṁ thērā ॥72 ।।
5 ukkhitta'paccavāē kaṁḍē pīsē va'chūḍha-bhajjantī ।
sukkaṁ va pōsamāṇī buddhīya vibhāvaē sammaṁ ।।73 ।।
kattaṁtīē thūlaṁ vivikhaṇa lōḍhaṇa jati ya niviyaṁ ।
piṁjaṇa asōyavāī bhayaṇāgahaṇaṁ tu ēēsi ।। 74 ।।
gamaṇaṁ ca dāyagassā hēṭṭhā uri ca hōi nāyavvaṁ ।
10 saṁjamanāyavirāhaṇa tassa sarīrē ya micchattaṁ ।। 75 ।।
nōyaduvārugghāḍaṇa-kavāḍaṭhiya dēha dāramāinnē ।
iḍḍirapatthiyalidē gahaṇaṁ pattassa'paḍilēhā ।। 76 ।।
āgamaṇadāyagassā hēṭṭhā uri ca hōi jaha puṭviṁ ।
saṁjamaāyavirāhaṇa diḷaṁtō hōi vacchēṇa ॥ 77 ।।
pattassa u paḍilēhā hatthē matsē tahēva davē ya ।
udaullē sasiṇiddha saṁsattē cēva pariyatē ॥ 78 ।।
paḍiō khalu davvō kittima sāhāvimō ya jō piḍō।
saṁjamanāyavirāhaṇa disetō siṭriṭhakabbō ॥79 ।।
garavisa aṭhiyakaṁṭaya-viruddha-davvaṁmi hōi āyāē ।
20 saṁjamaō chakāyā tamhā paḍiyaṁ vigicijjā ।। 480 ।।
aṇabhōgēṇa bhaēṇa ya paḍiṇī ummīsa bhattapāṇaṁmi ।
dijjā hiraṇṇamāī āvajjaṇa saṁkaṇā diṭhē ।। 81 ।।

[ niyuktisaṁgrahā :: (2) śrīmatī ōghaniyuktiḥ
iya ālōiya-paṭṭavina-gāliē maṁḍalīi saṭṭāṇē ।
sajjhāyamaṁgalaṁ kuṇai jāva samvē paḍiniyattā ॥559 ।।
kālapurisē va prāsajja mattaē pavikhavittu tō paḍhamā ।
ahavāvi paḍiggahagaṁ muti gacchaṁ samāsajja ।। 560 ।।
5 cittaṁ bālāīṇaṁ gahāya āpucchiūṇa āyariaṁ ।
jamalajaṇaṇīsaricchō nivēsaī maṁḍalīthērō ।। 561 ॥
jai luddhō rāiṇipō hōi aluddhōvi jō'vi gōyatyō !
ōmōvi hu gīyatthō maṁḍalirāiṇi praluddhō u ।।562 ।।
ṭhāṇavisi pagāsaragayā bhāyaṇa pakkhēvaṇā ya bhāva gurū ।
10 sō cēva ya ālōgō nāraṇattaṁ taddisāṭhāṇē ।। 563 ।।
jō puṇa havējja khamanō atiuccāmō va sō bahi ṭhāi ।
paḍhamasamuddiṭṭhō vā sāgāriyarakṣaṇāē ॥ 564 ।।
ēkkēkassa ya pāsaṁmi mallayaṁ tattha khēlamuggālē ।
kaṭhṭhiē va chumbhai mā lēvakaḍā bhavē vasahī ।। 565 ।।
15 maṁḍalibhāyaṇabhōyaṇa gahaṇaṁ sōhī ya kāraṇudhvaritē ।
bhōyaṇavihī u ēsō bhaṇiō tēllukkadaṁsīhi ।। 566 ।।
uggama-uppāyaṇāsuddhaṁ, ēsaṇā dōsavajjinaṁ ।
sāhāraṇaṁ ayāṇaṁtō, sāhū havai asāraō ॥ 567 ।।
uggama-upāyaṇāsuddhaṁ ēsaṇā-dōsavajjinaṁ ।

nāsaṁti caraṇakaraṇaṁ bāhirakaraṇālasā kēi ।। 61 ।।
ēvamiṇaṁ uvagaraṇaṁ dhārēmāṇō vihīsuparisuddhaṁ ।
hati guṇāṇāyataṇaṁ avihi asuddhē aṇāyayaṇaṁ ।। 62 ।।
sāvajjamaṇāyataṇaṁ asōhiṭhāṇaṁ kusīlasaṁsaggī ।
ēgaṭṭhā hōti padā ētē vivarīya āyayaṇā ।। 63 ।।
vajjēttu aṇāyataṇaṁ prāyataṇagavēsaṇaṁ sayā kujjā ।
taṁ tu puṇa aṇāyayaṇaṁ nāyavvaṁ dasvabhāvēṇaṁ ॥ 64 ।।
davvē ruddāigharā aṇāyataṇaṁ bhāvanō duvihamēva ।
20 lōiya lōguttariyaṁ tahiyaṁ puṇa lōiyaṁ iṇamō ।। 65 ॥
khariyā tirikkhajōṇī tālayara samaṇa māhaṇa susāṇē ।
vagguriya vāha gummiya hariēsa puliṁda macchaṁdhā ॥ 66 ।।

10 āhākamma paḍuccā niyamā sunō carimabhaṁgō ॥ 34 ।।
iṁdatthaṁ jaha sadā puraṁdarāī u nāivattāṁtē ।
ahakamma āyahammā taha māhaṁ nāivattē ।। 35 ।।
āhākammēṇa ahēkarēti jaṁ haṇai pāṇabhūyāī ।
jaṁ taṁ prāyayamāṇō parakamma attaṇō kuṇai ।। 36 ॥
15 kassatti pucchiyaṁmī niyamā sāhammiyasma ta hōi ।
sāhammiyassa tamhā
parūvaṇā vihiṇā
(parūvaṇaṁ tassa vōcchāmi) ।। 37 ।।
nāmaṁ ṭhavaṇā daviē khēttē kālē a pavayaṇē ligē।
dasaṇa-nāṇa carittē abhiggahē bhāvaṇāō ya ॥ 38 ॥
20 nāmaṁmi sarisanāmō ṭhavaṇāē kāṭakammamāīyā ।
davvaṁmi jō u bhaviō sāhami sarīragaṁ cēva ॥ 39 ॥
khēttē samāṇadēsī kālaṁmi samāṇakālasaṁbhūō ।
pavayaṇi saṁghēgayarō ligē rayaharaṇamuhapōttī ॥140 ।।
kāyadava

dasaṇa nāṇē caraṇē tiga paṇa paṇa tiviha hōi u carittē।
davvāinō abhiggaha aha bhāvaṇamō aṇiccāī ॥ 41 ।।
jāvaṁta dēvadattā gihīva agihīva tēsi dāhāmi ।

15 nāṇacarittā ēvaṁ nāyavyā hōṁti pavayaṇēṇaṁ tu ।

liṁgāīhivi ēvaṁ ēkkēkēṇaṁ tu uvarimā nēyā ।

10

ēvaṁ kaḍē ya kammē ēkkēvika caukkaō bhēō ॥ 26 ॥

samaṇāṇaṁ āēsaṁ niggaṁthāṇaṁ samāēsaṁ ।। 230 ॥
5 chinnamachinnaṁ duvihaṁ davē khēttē ya kāla bhāvē ya ।
niṣphāiyanipphannaṁ nāyavvaṁ jaṁ jahiṁ kamai ।। 31 ।।
mattuvariyaṁ khalu saṁkhaḍīēm̐ taddivasamannadivasē vā।
aṁtō bahiṁ ca savvaṁ savvadiṇaṁ dēhi pracchinnaṁ ॥ 32 ॥
dēhi imaṁ mā sēsaṁ aṁtō bāhiraggayaṁ va ēgayaraṁ ।
jāva pramugattivēlā amugaṁ vēlaṁ ca prārambha ।। 33 ।।
davvāīchinnapi hu jai bhaṇaī prāraō'vi mā dēha ।
tō kappai chinnapi hu acchinnakaḍaṁ pariharaṁti ।। 34 ।।
amugāṇaṁti va dijjau amukāṇaṁ matti ēttha u vibhāsā ।
jattha jaīṇa visiṭṭhō niddēsō taṁ pariharaṁti ॥ 35 ।।
15 saṁdissaṁtaṁ jō suṇai kappaē tassa sēsa ē ṭhavaṇā ।
saṁkaliya sāhaṇaṁ vā karēṁti asuē imā mērā ।। 36 ।।
mā ēyaṁ dēhi imaṁ puḍhē siṭṭhami taṁ pariharaṁti ।
jaṁ dinnaṁ taṁ dinnaṁ mā saṁpai dēhi gēṇhati ।। 37 ॥
rasabhāyaṇahēuṁ vā mā kucchihiī suhaṁ va dāhāmi ।
20 dahimāī āyataṁ karēi kūraṁ kaḍaṁ ēyaṁ ।। 38 ।।
mā kāhaṁti avaṇaṁ parikaliyaṁ va dijjai suhaṁ tu ।
viyaḍēṇa phāṇiēṇa va niddhēṇa samaṁ tu vaṭuṁti ।। 36 ।।

dōni u sāhusamutthā saṁkiya taha bhāvanō'pariṇayaṁ ca ।

nāma ṭhavaṇā daviē bhāvē gahaṇēsaṇā muṇēyavvā ।
davē vānarajahaṁ bhāvaṁmi ya dasa payā hum̐ti ।। 16 ।।
15 parisaḍiya-paṁḍupattaṁ vaṇasaṁḍaṁ daṭṭa annahiṁ pēsē ।

viyarai tēsi payāraṁ cariūṇa ya tō dahaṁ gacchē ।। 18 ।।
ōyaraṁtaṁ payaṁ dadru, nīharaṁtaṁ na dīsaī ।

dadhvaṁmi hōi chakkaṁ bhāvaṁmi ya hōi sajhilagā ।। 606 ।।
5 jīvattami avigaē apariṇayaṁ pariṇayaṁ gaē jīvē ।
di8tō duddhadahī iya apariṇaya pariṇayaṁ taṁ ca ।। 610 ।।
dugamāī sāmannē jai pariṇamaī u tattha ēgasta ।
dēmitti na sēsāṇaṁ apariṇayaṁ bhāvō ēyaṁ ।। 11 ।।
ēgēṇa vāvi ēsi maṇami pariṇāmiyaṁ na iyarēṇaṁ ।
10 taṁpi hu hōi agijjha sajhilagā sāmi sāhū vā ।। 12 ।।
ghēttavva-malēvakaḍaṁ lēvakaḍē mā hu pacchakammāī ।
na ya rasagēhipasaṁgō ina vuttē cōyagō bhaṇai ।। 13 ॥
jai pacchakammadōsā havaṁti mā cēva bhujaū sayayaṁ ।
tavaniyama-saṁjamāṇaṁ cōyaga! hāṇī khamaṁtassa ।। 14 ।।
15 littaṁti bhāṇiūṇa chammāsā hāyaē cautthaṁ tu
āyaṁbilassa gahaṇaṁ asaṁtharē prappalēvaṁ tu ।। 15 ।
prāyaṁbila-pāraṇaē chammāsa niraṁtaraṁ tu khaviūṇaṁ ।
jai na tarai chammāsē ēgadiṇūṇaṁ taō kuṇau ।। 16 ।।
ēvaṁ ēkkēkkadiṇaṁ āyaṁbilapāraṇaṁ khavēūṇaṁ ।
20 divasē divasē giṇhau āyaṁbilamēva nillēvaṁ ।। 17 ।।
jai sē na jōgahāṇī saṁpai ēsē va hōi tō khamaō।
khamaṇaṁtarēṇa āyaṁbilaṁ tu niyayaṁ tavaṁ kuṇai ।। 18 ।।

5
ahigammati va atthā imēṇa ahiga ca nayaṇamicchati ।
ahigaṁ ca sāhū gacchai tamhā ajjhayaṇamicchati ।। 30 ।।

nāṇassa daṁsaṇastavi caraṇassa va jēṇa āgamō hōī ।
sō hōi bhāvaāō āō lāhō tti niddiṭṭō ।। 32 ॥
pradavihaṁ kammarayaṁ pōrāṇaṁ jaṁ khavēi jōgēhi ।
ēvaṁ bhāvajjhayagaṁ nēprabvaṁ āṇupuvīē ।। 33 ।।
ṇāmadumō ṭhavaṇadumō davadumō cēva hōi bhāvadumō।
10 ēmēva ya puṣphassa vi ca uṭhivahō hōi nikkhēvō ॥ 34 ॥
dumā ya pāyavā rukkhā, agamā viḍimā tarū ।
kuhā mahīruhā vacchā, rōvagā rujagāvi pra॥ 35 ।।
pupphāriṇa prakusumāṇi a pullāṇi tahēva hōṁti pasavāṇi ।
sumaṇāriṇa a suhamāṇi a pupphāṇaṁ hōṁti ēgaṭṭhā ।। 36 ।।
15 dumapulphimā ya māhāraēsaṇā gōarē tayā uṁchō ।
mēsa jalūgā sappē vaṇa'vakhaisugōlaputtudaē ।। 37 ।।
katthai pucchaha sīsō kahiṁca'puṭṭhā kahaṁti āyariyā।
sīsāṇaṁ tu hiyaṭṭhā vipulatarāgaṁ tu pucchāē ।॥ 38 ॥
ṇāmaṁṭhavaṇadhammō damvadhammō prabhāvadhammō pra ।
20 ēēsi nāṇataṁ vucchāmi prahāṇupuvīē ।। 39 ।।
davvaṁ ca asthikāyappayāradhammō prabhāvadhammō a ।
davassa pajjavā jē tē dhammā tassa dadhvassa ॥ 40 ।।

mattaṁ sahāvasiddhaṁ samaṇasuvihiyā gavēsaṁti ॥ 28 ।।
5 upasaṁhārō bhamarā jaha taha samaṇāvi pravahajīvitti ।
daṁtatti puṇa payaṁmī nāyavvaṁ dhakkasēsamiṇaṁ ।। 29 ।।
jaha istha cēva iriyāiēsu savvaṁmi dikkhiyapayārē ।
tasathāvarabhūyahiyaṁ jayaṁti sammādhiyaṁ sāhū ॥130 ॥
uvasahāravisuddhī ēsa samattā u nigamaṇaṁ tēṇaṁ ।
10 vaccati sāhuṇōtti (ya) jēṇaṁ tē mahuyarasamāṇā ।। 31 ।।
tamhā dayāiguṇasuṭṭhiēhiṁ bhamarōvva avaha vittīhi ।
sāhahiṁ sāhiu tti ukkiḷaṁ maṁgalaṁ dhammō ।। 32 ।।
nigamaṇasuddhī tityaṁtarāvi dhammasthamujjayā viharē ।
bhaṇṇai kāyāṇaṁ tē jayaṇaṁ na murṇati na karēṁti ॥ 33 ॥
na ya uggamāisuddhaṁ bhujaṁtī mahuyarā va'ṇuvarōhī ।
nēva ya tiguttiguttā jaha sāhū niccakālaṁpi ॥ 34 ॥
kāyaṁ vāyaṁ ca maṇaṁ ca iṁdiyāī ca paṁca damayaṁti ।
dhārēṁti baṁbhacēraṁ saṁjamayaṁti kasāē ya ॥ 35 ॥
jaṁ ca tavē ujjuttā tēṇēsiṁ sāhulakkhaṇaṁ puṇṇaṁ ।
20 tō sāhuṇō ti bhaṇṇati sāhavō nigamaṇaṁ cēyaṁ ।। 36 ।।
tē u painna vibhattī hēu vibhattī vivakkhapaḍisēhō ।
di→tō āsaṁkā tappaḍisēhō nigamaṇaṁ ca ॥ 37 ।।

>
kaḍaē tē kuṁḍalē ya tē, aṁjiyakkhi ! tilayatē ya tē ।

itthaṁ puṇa ahigārō ṇāyavō hōi maṇupramaraṇēṇaṁ ।
muttu akāmamaraṇaṁ sakāmamaraṇēṇa mariyavvaṁ ॥ 234 ।।
॥ iti pañcamādhyayananiyuktiḥ ॥ 5 ॥
॥ 6॥ atha ṣaṣṭakṣullaka nigranthīyādhyayananiryaktiḥ ॥
nāma ṭhavaṇā daviē khittē kālē pahāṇa pai bhāvō ।
ēēsi mahaṁtāṇaṁ paḍivakkhō khullayā huti ॥235 ॥
nikkhēvō niyaṁṭhami cauvihō duvihō ya davbaṁmi ।
āgamanōāgamaō nōāgamatō ya sō tivihō ।। 36 ।।
jāṇagasarīrabhaviē tavvatirittē ya niṇhagāīsu।
bhāmi niyaṁṭhō khalu paṁcavihō hōi nāyavō ।। 37 ॥
ukkōsō u niyaṁṭhō jahannō cēva hōi ṇāyacō ।
ajahannamaṇukkōsā huṁti niyaṁṭhā asaṁkhijjā ॥ 38 ।।
15 duvihō ya hōi gaṁthō bajjhō abhitarō ya nāyavō।
aṁtō ya ca udasavihō dasahā puṇa bāhirō gaṁthō ।। 39 ।।
kōhō māṇō māyā lōbhē pijjē tahēva dōsē ya ।
micchatta vēna arai rai hāsa sōgē ya duggaṁchā ॥ 240 ॥
khēttaṁ vatthū dhaṇadhannasaṁcaō mittanāisaṁjōgō ।
jāṇasayaraṇāsaṇāṇi a dāsīdāsaṁ ca kuviyaṁ ca ।। 41 ।।

lakṣaṇamēvaṁ cēva u payarassa asaṁkhabhāgamittā u ।
nikkhamaṇē ya pavēsē ēgāīyāvi ēmēva ॥ 58 ।।
5 nikkhamapavēsakālō samayāī ittha āvalībhāgō।
aṁtōmuttavirahō udahisahassāhiē dōnni ।। 56 ।। dāraṁ ।।
maṁsāīparibhōgō satthaṁ satthāiyaṁ aṇēgavihaṁ ।
sārīramāṇasā vēyaṇā ya duvihā bahuvihā ya ।।160॥ dāraṁ ।।
maṁsassa kēi aṭṭhā kēi cammassa kēi rōmāṇaṁ ।
10 picchāṇaṁ pucchāṇaṁ daṁtāṇa'ṭṭhā vahijjati ।। 61 ।।
kē ī vahaṁti aṭṭhā kēi aṇaṭṭā pasaṁgadōsēṇaṁ ।
kammapasagapasattā baṁdhati vahati māraṁti ।। 62 ।।
sēsāī dārāī tāī jāi havaṁti puḍhavīē ।
ēvaṁ tasakāyamī nijjuttī kittiyā ēsā ॥ 163 ।।
15 ॥1-7॥ atha prathamādhyayanē saptamavāyukāyōddēśakaḥ ॥
vāussa'vi dārāī tāī jāī havaṁti puḍhavīē ।
nāṇattī u vihāṇē parimāṇuvabhōgasatthēya ।। 164 ।।
duvihā ya vāujīvā suhumā taha bāyarā u lōgaṁmi ।
suhumā ya sabalōē paṁcēva ya bāyaravihāṇā ।। 65 ।।
20 ukkaliyā maṁḍaliyā guṁjā ghaṇavāya suddhavāyā ya ।
bāyaravāuvihāṇā paṁcavihā vaṇiyā ēē । 66 ।।

caiūṇaṁ saṁkapayaṁ sārapayamiṇaṁ daḍhēṇa cittavvaṁ ।

lōgē caubdhihamī samaṇassa caudivahō kahaṁ cārō? ।

pāvōvaraē apariggahē a gurukulanisēvaē juttē ।
ummaggavajjaē rāgadōsaviraē ya sē viharē ॥ 248 ।।

pāhaṇṇē parimāṇē ya chavihō hōi nikkhēvō ।। 1 ।।
10 davē khēttē kālē bhāvaṁmi ya hōṁti yā pahāṇā u !
tēsi mahāsaddō khalu pāhaṇṇēṇaṁ tu niṣphannō ।। 2 ।।
davē khēttē kālē bhāmi ya jē bhavē mahaṁtā u ।
tēsu mahāsaddō khalu pamāṇaō hōṁti nipphannō ।। 3 ।।
davvē khēttē kālē bhāvapariṣṇā ya hōḍa bōddhavvā ।
15 jāṇaṇanōvavavakhaṇaō ya duvihā puṇēkkēkkā ।। 4 ।।
bhāvariṣṇā duvihā mūlaguṇa cēva uttaraguṇē ya ।
mūlaguṇē paṁcavihā duvihā puṇa uttaraguṇēsu ।। 5 ।।
pāhaṇṇaṇa u pagayaṁ pariṇāē ya tahaya duvihāē ।
pariṇāṇēsu pahāṇē mahāpariṇā taō hōi ।। 6 ।।
20 dēvīṇaṁ maṇuīṇaṁ tirikkhajōṇīgayāṇa itthīṇaṁ ।
tivihēṇa pariccāprō mahāpariṇāē nijjuttī ॥ 7 ॥
॥ iti mahāpariṇānijjutti ।।

॥7॥ śrī sūtrakr̥tāṅganiyuktiḥ ॥
॥ sūtrakr̥tāṅgōpōdghātaniyuktiḥ ।।
tittha yarē ya jiṇavarē suttakarē gaṇaharē ya gamiūṇaṁ ।
sūyagaḍassa bhagavaō ṇijjukti kittaissāmi ॥1॥
sūyagaḍaṁ aṁgāṇaṁ bitiyaṁ tassa ya imāṇi nāmāṇi ।
sūtagaḍaṁ suttakaḍaṁ sūyagaḍaṁ cēva gōṇṇāiṁ ॥2॥
davvaṁ tu pōṇḍayādī bhāvē suttamiha sūyagaṁ nāṇaṁ ।
saṇṇāsaṁgahavittē jātiṇibaddha ya katthādī ।। 3 ।।
karaṇaṁ ca kāraō ya kaḍaṁ ca tiṇhapi chakkanikkhēvō ।
10 davē khittē kālē bhāvēṇa u kāraō jīvō ॥4॥
davvaṁ paōgavīsasa paōgasā mūla uttarē cēva ।
uttarakaraṇaṁ vaṁjaṇa atthō u uvakkharō samvō ॥ 5 ॥
mūlakaraṇaṁ sarīrāṇi paṁca tisu karaṇakhaṁdhamādīyaṁ ।
dadhviṁdiyāṇi pariṇāmiyāṇi visanōsahādīhiṁ ।। 6 ।।
15 saṁghāyaṇē ya parisāḍaṇā ya mīsē tahēva paḍisēhō।
paḍasaṁkhasagaḍathūṇāuḍḍhatiricchādikaraṇaṁ ca ॥7 ।।
khaṁdhēsu duppaēsādiēsu prabhēsu vijjumāīsu ।
ṇipphagṇagāṇi davvāṇi jāṇa taṁ vīsasākaraṇaṁ ॥ 8 ॥
ṇa viṇā prāgāsēṇaṁ kīraija kici khēttamāgāsaṁ ।
20 vaṁjaṇapariyāvaṇa ucchukaraṇamādiyaṁ bahuhā ॥ 6 ।।

kālō jō jāvaiō jaṁ kōrai jaṁmi jaṁmi kālaṁmi ।

bhāvē u ōhasīlaṁ abhikkhamāsēvaṇā cēva ॥ 86 ।।
ōhē sīlaṁ viratī virayāviraī ya aviratī asōlaṁ ।
15 dhammē jāṇatavādī apasastha ahammakōvādī ।। 87 ।।
paribhāsiyā kusīlā ya ēttha jāvaṁti aviratā kēī ।
sutti pasaṁsā suddhō kutti duguṁchā aparisuddhō ॥ 88 ॥
aphāsuyapaḍisēviya ṇāmaṁ bhujjō ya sīlavādī ya ।
phāsu vayaṁti sōlaṁ aphāsuyā mō abhujaṁtā ।। 89 ।।
jaha ṇāma gōyamā caṁḍīdēvagā vāribhaddagā cēva ।
jē agnihōttavādī jalasōyaṁ jē ya icchati ॥ 60 ।

taṁ nēi pitā tōsē pucchaṇa kahaṇaṁ ca varaṇa dōvārē ।

5
॥1॥ prathamā samādhisthānādhyayananiryaktiḥ ।।
vaṁdāmi bhaddayāhuṁ pāīṇaṁ carimasayalasuyanāṇi ।
suttassa kāraṇamisi dasāsu kappē ya vavahārē ॥1॥
āu vivāgajjhayaṇāṇi bhāvaō daśvaō u vasthadasā ।
dasaāō vivāgadasā vāsasayāō dasahacchēttā ।। 2 ।।
bālā maṁdā kiḍḍā balā ya paṇṇā ya hāyaṇipavaṁcā।
panbhāramummuhī sayaṇī nāmēhi ya lakkhaṇēhi dasā ।। 3 ।।
dasāmrō vivāgadasā nāmēhi ya lakkhaṇēhi ēhiti ।
10 ēttō ajjhayaṇadasā ahakkama kittaissāmi ।। 4 ।।
ḍaharīō u imāō ajjayaṇēsu mahaīō aṁgēsu ।
chasu nāyādīēsu vayavibhūsāvasāṇamiva ।।5।।
ḍaharīō u imāō nijjūḍhāō aṇuggahaṭṭāē ।
thērēhiṁ tu dasāō jō dasā jāṇaō jīvō।। 6 ।।
15 asamāhi ya sabalataṁ aṇasādaṇagaṇiguṇā maṇasamāhī।
sāvagabhikkhūpaḍimā kappō mōhō niyāṇaṁ ca
dasāṇaṁ piṁḍasthō ēsō mē vaṇṇiō samāsēṇaṁ ।
ētō ēkkēkkaṁpi ya ajjhayaṇaṁ kittaissāmi ॥ 8 ॥
davvaṁ jēṇa va damvēṇa samāhī āhiyaṁ ca jaṁ dadhvaṁ ।
bhāvō susamāhitayā jīvassa pasatyajōgēhiṁ ।। 9 ।।

cikkhala vāsa rōhēṇa vā vi tēṇa ṭṭhiyā ūṇā ॥ 59 ।।
vāsākhēttālabhē addhāṇādīsu pattamahigātō ।
10 sāhagavāghāēṇa va prapaḍikkamiuṁ jai vayaṁti ।। 60 ।।
paḍimāpaḍivāṇaṁ ēgāhaṁ paṁca hōta'hālaṁdē ।
jiṇasuddhāṇaṁ māsō nikkāraṇaō ya thērāṇaṁ ।। 61 ।।
ūṇāiritta māsā ēvaṁ thērāṇa prakr̥ ṇāyavvā ।
iyarē aṭṭa vihariu ṇiyamā cattāri acchanti ।। 62 ।।
15 āsāḍhapuṣṇimāē vāsāvāsaṁtu hōti gatavvaṁ ।
maggasirabahuladasamīu jāva ēkkammi khēttammi ।। 63 ।।
bāhi ṭhittati vasahiṁ khēttaṁ gāhēttu vāsapāōggaṁ ।
kappaṁ kahēttu ṭhavaṇā sāvaṇa suddhassa paṁcāhē ।। 64 ।।
ēttha tu aṇabhiggahiyaṁ vīsatirāyaṁ savīsatīmāsaṁ ।
20 tēṇa paramabhiggahiraṁ gihiṇātaṁ kattiō jāva ।। 65 ।।
asivāikāraṇēhiṁ ahavā vāsaṁ suṭhṭha āraddhaṁ ।
ahivaḍiyammi vīsā iyarēsu savīsaī māsō ॥ 66 ।।

(8) śrōdaśāśrutaskaṁdhaniyuktiḥ ]
[ 483
5
ēttha tu paṇagaṁ paṇagaṁ kāraṇiyaṁ jā savīsatīmāsō।
suddhadasamīṭṭhiyāṇa va āsāḍhīpuṇimōsaraṇaṁ ।। 67 ।।
iya sattarī jahaṇṇā asīti ṇautī dasuttarasayaṁ ca ।
jai vāsati miggasirē dasarāyā tiṇi ukkōsā ।। 68 ॥
kāūraṇa māsakappaṁ tatthēva ṭhiyāṇa'tīē maggasīrē ।
sālambaṇāṇa chammāsitō tu jaṭṭhōggahō hōti ।। 66 ।।
jai asthi payavihārō caupaḍivayammi hōi gaṁtavvaṁ ।
ahavāvi aṇitassā ārōvaṇapuvaniddiṭṭhā ॥70 ।।
kāīyabhūmī saṁthāraē ya saṁsatta dullahē bhikkhē ।
10 ēēhiṁ kāraṇēhi apattē hōi niggamaṇaṁ ।। 71 ।।
rāyā sappē kuthū agaṇi gilāṇē ya thaṁḍilassa'sati ।
ēēhi kāraṇēhi apattē hōi niggamaṇaṁ ।। 72 ।।
vāsaṁ va na ōrabhaī paṁthā vā duggamā sacikhallā।
ēēhi kāraṇēhi aikkatē hōi niggamaṇaṁ ।। 73 ।।
15 asivē ōmōyariē rāyā duṭhē bhaē va gēlaṇṇē ।
ēēhi kāraṇēhi praikatē hōti niggamaṇaṁ ।। 74 ।।
ubhaōvi addhajōyaṇa saaddhakōsaṁ ca taṁ habati khēttaṁ ।
hōi sakōsaṁ jōyaṇa, mōtūṇa kāraṇajjāē ।। 75 ।।
uḍḍamahē tiriyammi ya, sakōsayaṁ samvatō havati khēttaṁ ।
20 iṁdapayamāiēsu chaddisi iyarēsu cau paca ।। 76 ।।
tiṇi duvē ēkkā vā vādhāēṇaṁ disā havai khēttaṁ ।
ujjāṇāprō parēṇaṁ chiṇṇamaṁḍavaṁ tu akhēttaṁ ।। 77 ।।
